   tatpūjāharahaḥ paścāttadgrāmasya vināśakṛt // Vis_39.333 //	tad pUjA harahaH paScAt tad grAmasya vinASa kRt // ViH _39.333 //
   tasmāt sarvaprayatnena pūjayettaddvijottama /	tasmAt sarva prayatnena pUjayet tat dvijottamaH /
   pūrvaṃ karmārcanādīnāṃ śuddhasnānaṃ tu kārayet // Vis_39.334 //	pUrvam karma arcana AdInAm SudDa snAnam tu kArayet // ViH _39.334 //
   jalasaṃprokṣaṇādīni mūlārcāyāṃ niyojayet /	jala saMprokzaNa AdIni mUla arcAyAm niyojayet /
   snapanādīni karmāṇi karmārcāyāṃ niyojayet // Vis_39.335 //	snapana AdIni karmANi karma arcAyAm niyojayet // ViH _39.335 //
   utsavaṃ kārayettasmin balihomapuraḥsaram /	utsavam kArayet tasmin bali homa puraHsaram /
   ekāhaṃ vā tryahaṃ vātha saptāhaṃ vā munīśvara // Vis_39.336 //	eka aham vA tri aham vA aTa sapta aham vA muni ISvaraH // ViH _39.336 //
   kārayedutsavaṃ tatra yathāśaktyānurūpataḥ (!) /	kArayet utsavam tatra yaTASaktyA anurUpatas (!) /
   etat krameṇa kartavyaṃ dvādaśābdāntameva ca // Vis_39.337 //	etat krameNa kartavyam dvAdaSa abda antam eva ca // ViH _39.337 //
   ekābde rakṣasāṃ sthānaṃ (vāsaḥ?) tasmācchāntiṃ tu kāreyat /	eka abde rakzasAm sTAnam (vAsaH?) tasmAt SAntim tu kAreyat /
   dvyabde ca yakṣavāsastu tryabde bhūtasaṃkulam // Vis_39.338 //	dvi abde ca yakza vAsaH tu tri abde BUta saMkulam // ViH _39.338 //
   caturabde piśācānāṃ pañcābde dānavālayam /	catur abde piSAcAnAm paQca abde dAnava Alayam /
   pañcavarṣamatīte tu nivāso brahmarakṣasām // Vis_39.339 //	paQca varzam atIte tu nivAsaH brahma rakzasAm // ViH _39.339 //
   tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kṣipraṃ śāntiṃ tu kārayet /	tasmAt sarva prayatnena kzipram SAntim tu kArayet /
   dvādaśābdāt purā kuryāt jalasaṃprokṣaṇena tu // Vis_39.340 //	dvAdaSa abdAt purA kuryAt jala saMprokzaNena tu // ViH _39.340 //
   evameva tu kartavyaṃ viṃśadvarṣāntameva tu /	evam eva tu kartavyam viMSat varza antam eva tu /
   ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittaṃ tu nārada // Vis_39.341 //	atas param pravakzyAmi prAyaScittam tu nAradaH // ViH _39.341 //
   jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kuryājjalavāsapuraḥsaram /	jala saMprokzaNam kuryAt jala vAsa puraHsaram /
   brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścānmahāhavipuraḥsaram // Vis_39.342 //	brAhmaNAn Bojayet paScAt mahA Ahavi puraHsaram // ViH _39.342 //
   ṣaṭtriṃśadvatsarādarvāk tāvattenaiva kārayet /	zawtriMSat vatsarAt arvAk tAvat tena eva kArayet /
   ṣaṭtriṃśadvatsarādūrdhvaṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate // Vis_39.343 //	zawtriMSat vatsarAt UrDvam prAyaScittam viDIyate // ViH _39.343 //
   pañcagavyaṃ kramāt kṛtvā garbhāgāraṃ viśodhayet /	paQcagavyam kramAt kRtvA garBAgAram viSoDayet /
   puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu brāhmaṇānāmanujñayā // Vis_39.344 //	puNya aham vAcayitvA tu brAhmaNAnAm anujQayA // ViH _39.344 //
   jalādhivāsanādīni pūrvoktenaiva kārayet /	jala aDivAsana AdIni pUrva uktena eva kArayet /
   godānaṃ bhūmidānaṃ ca hiraṇyaṃ vastrameva ca // Vis_39.345 //	go dAnam BUmi dAnam ca hiraNyam vastram eva ca // ViH _39.345 //
   sarvadānaṃ tataḥ kuryāt brāhmaṇebhyo yathākramam /	sarva dAnam tatas kuryAt brAhmaNeByaH yaTAkramam /
   evaṃ tadvardhayitvā tu pañcāśadvatsarāntakam // Vis_39.346 //	evam tat varDayitvA tu paQcASat vatsara antakam // ViH _39.346 //
   pañcāśadvatsarādūrdhvāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate /	paQcASat vatsarAt UrDvAm prAyaScittam viDIyate /
   jalādhivāsanādīni punaḥ sthāpanamārabhet // Vis_39.347 //	jala aDivAsana AdIni punar sTApanam AraBet // ViH _39.347 //
   brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret /	brAhmaNAn Bojayet tatra Sezam pUrvavat Acaret /
   etat krameṇa kartavyaṃ śatavarṣāntameva ca // Vis_39.348 //	etat krameNa kartavyam Sata varza antam eva ca // ViH _39.348 //
   saṃvatsaraśatādūrdhvaṃ śūnyasthānaṃ bhaveddhruvam /	saMvatsara SatAt UrDvam SUnya sTAnam Bavet Druvam /
   tadgrāmaṃ nidhanaṃ yāti tatrasthā narakaṃ vrajet(?) // Vis_39.349 //	tad grAmam niDanam yAti tatrasTAH narakam vrajet (?) // ViH _39.349 //
   tadgrāmaṃ nidhanaṃ yāti tasmācchāntiṃ tu kārayet /	tad grAmam niDanam yAti tasmAt SAntim tu kArayet /
   śāntiṃ kṛtvā vidhānena pañcarātreṇa pūjayet // Vis_39.350 //	SAntim kRtvA viDAnena paQca rAtreNa pUjayet // ViH _39.350 //
   pūjālope 'pi cettasmin punastenaiva pūjayet /	pUjA lope api ced tasmin punar tena eva pUjayet /
   tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kṣipraṃ śāntiṃ samācaret // Vis_39.351 //	tasmAt sarva prayatnena kzipram SAntim samAcaret // ViH _39.351 //
   iti śrīpāñcarātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ prāyaścittavidhirnāma	iti SrI pAQcarAtre vizvaksena saMhitAyAm prAyaScittaviDiH nAma
   ekonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||	ekonacatvAriMSaH aDyAyaH ||
